msg:Yaojia is a national brand niche hotel/homestay group. There are currently 6 stores in the country, three of which are near the Huangguoshu Waterfall in Anshun. Wangpu and Fanshe are actually next to each other, so I only experienced the better Wangpu. The other waterfall village is directly in the scenic area, and is only separated by a wall from the national brand top luxury Bailian. From the picture, you can see that the two house numbers are next to each other.
.
This time I used the ğŸ¬ room voucher, 769 yuan also included a full meal, and when I arrived at the hotel, I was upgraded to a 98-square-meter deluxe courtyard king-size bed room, which is equivalent to staying in a private soup room for about 500 yuan. It can be said that the price-performance ratio is full. Note that the room types above this courtyard room are all equipped with private hot springs, and the deluxe courtyard big regular price booking is only about 1,400 yuan. Compared with the basic room type of Bailian next door of about 4,000 yuan, it can be said that the price-performance ratio is very high and can be used as a substitute for Bailian.
.
The hotel was originally an abandoned old house next to Bo Lian, and it can be regarded as a successful renovation project. Although the public area is not large, it is still very impressive, especially the courtyard with an infinity pool. As a small boutique hotel, it also provides 24-hour butler service with a fast response speed.
.
The deluxe courtyard room is nominally 98 square meters, which should be the area of â€‹â€‹the front and back yards. It is very close to the lobby, the gate and the restaurant, and there is no need to move luggage on the first floor. There is no landscape in the front yard. Entering the room is actually a large open space, with a double dining table at the door, a wardrobe and a mini bar, and then a bed. There is also a small table tatami near the backyard where you can sit around. There is no carpet in the whole house, and the wood is fresh. The facilities are still very new. There is a welcome fruit plate, handwritten cards, and a small refrigerator for free, but there are not many drinks. Loose tea is used, and there is no capsule coffee machine.
.
The backyard is quite large, and the outside of the wall is the landscape of the Park Lane. The area of â€‹â€‹the hot spring is good, and it feels slightly larger than the Park Lane suite. It can drain water automatically until it overflows, and the speed is very fast. The problem of insufficient hot water in the early days of opening should have been solved. In addition, my favorite thing is that the faucet of the hot spring can be rotated, so that you can easily clean the entire hot spring by just rotating the faucet.
.
The most important thing is that the privacy is guaranteed. I went to the second floor to visit several empty rooms that were being cleaned, including the aerial view, and the hot spring could not be seen at all. In fact, Park Lane is not as good at this.
.
The bathroom area is very spacious, with an artificial stone bathtub more than Park Lane. I have never seen the brand. The double basin is transparent and has a Toto washlet installed. The shower cylindrical shower head is installed too low, and the body feeling is average.
.
The service is good, the decoration is simple and elegant, and the location is excellent (you need to take a shuttle bus to get to the door from the guest room and lobby of Bo Lian, but it is only ten meters away from here). This private hot spring room is really cost-effective. If you book a basic room during the off-season, there is a high chance of upgrading. It is worth a try. I liked it even more when I stayed at their waterfall view room later. I will write about it slowly.

msg:The only advantage: the location is excellent, right next to the Great Falls Scenic Area, you can go to the scenic area early to avoid the crowds.
Problems:
1. The housekeeper contacted us in advance before check-in, but the feedback efficiency needs to be improved. He answered questions several times that were not asked. I had a bad impression before I checked in. The guy who came to the entrance of the scenic area didn't say a word after picking us up, and didn't even say goodbye when he sent us out when checking out. I wonder if he didn't pay enough?
2. Breakfast cannot be delivered to the room. The room lighting is dim, even when it is adjusted to the brightest, it is still dim. The night light is reddish, and the visual experience is not good. The welcome fruit is not very fresh and should have been placed for a while.
3. I confirmed with the housekeeper on WeChat whether I need to order in advance for dinner. He said that there is a temporary menu that can be ordered on the spot. I asked the front desk customer service when I checked in, and was told that the temporary menu can be ordered but I still need to wait for an hour. After booking a meal at 7 o'clock with the front desk, the housekeeper asked me on WeChat again after a while what time I need to eat.
4. There are hairs on the bed sheet when I lift it up. I don't know if it is changed for each guest. The shower water is not hot. There is only a little heat halfway through the shower, and it turns cold several times in the middle.
5. In the morning, I was going to the Great Falls scenic area. I met an employee at the entrance of the hotel. I wanted to ask which direction the ticket gate of the Great Falls should go. The answer was "It should be this direction." When asked about other scenic spots, the answer was "I don't know."
6. There is a self-service tea room written on the promotional page. At around 2 pm, there was still some time before the driver arrived. I wanted to take a rest. The front desk pointed us in a direction. After we went up with our luggage, it was completely impossible to stay inside. It was just a huge sun room without air conditioning. The two of us could only carry our things back to the lobby and sit. The front desk saw us coming down and turned a blind eye. When I was in the lobby, I heard other guests come out to question whether there was no room service. No one answered the phone, which shows that the service problem is not an isolated case.
In general, women's service is better than men's, but I still want to ask, whether it is breakfast or dinner during the stay, I only saw one or two tables of people. I donâ€™t know why the service is so bad when the occupancy rate is not high in the off-season?

msg:I thought for a long time about how to evaluate this hotel. First of all, this is a good-looking hotel. The boss is from Zhuji, Shaoxing, and he is a designer. Secondly, a common problem of homestays is that hygiene is not standardized, so hygiene still looks clean but there are many problems when you look closely. But the hotel has actively upgraded and improved. The overall accommodation is not bad. The rest is my travel suggestions: 1. Huangguoshu Scenic Area currently has three hotels in the core of the Big Waterfall (Big Waterfall is recommended, you can play even without water, Tianxing Bridge is similar to Shilin, and there is a steamed bun waterfall in Journey to the West. I personally think that you only need to see the Big Waterfall Scenic Area and have the Water Curtain Cave). It is said that you have to come even if you go down the mountain. They are all next to the Big Waterfall Scenic Area. Qianshou has the lowest grade but has a fast lane; Yaojia is second but has a small size, Bailian is large but expensive, and the cost-effectiveness is not high. The maintenance is very general; so I think the most cost-effective is Yaojia, and whether there is a fast lane really makes no difference to people living in the scenic area, just walk a little more. It is recommended to buy tickets for staying here, and you donâ€™t need to buy transportation to the scenic area. If you drive by yourself and just want to visit the Big Waterfall Scenic Area like me. Because you can drive to the hotel by car, if you don't drive by yourself or want to go to Tianxing Bridge, you still have to buy scenic area transportation. Many scenic spots have restrictions on foreign vehicles for money and safety reasons. Then you can drive in and out of the waterfall village scenic area unlimitedly. The two Internet celebrities who checked in Yaojia Anshun are Haowang Waterfall and Fanshe (Figure 3-4). In fact, they are next to each other with slightly different decorations. It is very worth checking in. Finally, I complain about the management of Huangguoshu. There are many points. It is still based on the principle of convenient management, which makes it inconvenient for many service personnel to enter and exit. However, if the service personnel are unhappy at work, it will affect the efficiency and service quality. They are exhausted when they walk in, so what are they doing? So it really still has to be based on the original, reduce unnecessary business, and do more management and beautification of the surrounding area.
